            // Wait for gtag to be available
            function waitForGtag(timeout = 10000) {
              return new Promise((resolve) => {
                if (typeof gtag === 'function') {
                  resolve(true);
                  return;
                }

                let attempts = 0;
                const maxAttempts = timeout / 100;

                const checkGtag = () => {
                  attempts++;
                  if (typeof gtag === 'function') {
                    resolve(true);
                  } else if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
                    resolve(false);
                  } else {
                    setTimeout(checkGtag, 100);
                  }
                };

                setTimeout(checkGtag, 100);
              });
            }

            // Promise helpers for GA4 session capture
            async function gtagGet(mid, field) {
              const gtagReady = await waitForGtag(5000);

              return new Promise((resolve) => {
                if (!gtagReady || typeof gtag !== 'function') {
                  resolve(null);
                  return;
                }

                try {
                  gtag('get', mid, field, (v) => resolve(v || null));

                  // Timeout fallback
                  setTimeout(() => resolve(null), 2000);
                } catch (e) {
                  resolve(null);
                }
              });
            }

            // Cookie extraction helpers
            function extractClientIdFromCookie() {
              try {
                const gaCookie = document.cookie
                  .split('; ')
                  .find(row => row.startsWith('_ga='));
                if (!gaCookie) return null;

                const parts = gaCookie.split('=')[1].split('.');
                return parts.length >= 4 ? parts[2] + '.' + parts[3] : null;
              } catch (e) {
                return null;
              }
            }

            function extractSessionIdFromCookie(measurementId) {
              try {
                const measurementIdSuffix = measurementId.startsWith('G-')
                  ? measurementId.substring(2)
                  : measurementId;

                const sessionCookie = document.cookie
                  .split('; ')
                  .find(row => row.startsWith('_ga_' + measurementIdSuffix + '='));

                if (!sessionCookie) return null;

                const cookieValue = sessionCookie.split('=')[1];

                // Handle GS2 format
                if (cookieValue.startsWith('GS2.1.')) {
                  const parts = cookieValue.substring(6).split('$');
                  const sessionPart = parts.find(part => part.startsWith('s'));
                  return sessionPart ? sessionPart.substring(1) : null;
                }

                // Handle GA1 format
                if (cookieValue.startsWith('GA1.1.')) {
                  const parts = cookieValue.split('.');
                  return parts.length >= 5 ? parts[4] : null;
                }

                return null;
              } catch (e) {
                return null;
              }
            }

            // Capture GA4 IDs (gtag first, cookie fallback)
            async function captureGa4Ids(measurementId) {
              let clientId = null;
              let sessionId = null;
              let sessionNumber = null;

              // Try gtag method first (with timeout)
              try {
                const gtagPromises = await Promise.allSettled([
                  gtagGet(measurementId, 'client_id'),
                  gtagGet(measurementId, 'session_id'),
                  gtagGet(measurementId, 'session_number'),
                ]);

                clientId = gtagPromises[0].status === 'fulfilled' ? gtagPromises[0].value : null;
                sessionId = gtagPromises[1].status === 'fulfilled' ? gtagPromises[1].value : null;
                sessionNumber = gtagPromises[2].status === 'fulfilled' ? gtagPromises[2].value : null;
              } catch (e) {
                // gtag failed, will fall back to cookies
              }

              // Cookie fallbacks
              if (!clientId) {
                clientId = extractClientIdFromCookie();
              }

              if (!sessionId) {
                sessionId = extractSessionIdFromCookie(measurementId);
              }

              return { clientId, sessionId, sessionNumber };
            }

            // Main function to get GA4 session data for cart
            window.getGa4SessionForCart = async function(measurementId) {
              try {
                const ids = await captureGa4Ids(measurementId);

                // Get UTM parameters from current URL
                const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
                const utmData = {
                  utmSource: urlParams.get('utm_source'),
                  utmMedium: urlParams.get('utm_medium'),
                  utmCampaign: urlParams.get('utm_campaign'),
                  utmTerm: urlParams.get('utm_term'),
                  utmContent: urlParams.get('utm_content'),
                  gclid: urlParams.get('gclid'),
                  fbclid: urlParams.get('fbclid'),
                  gad_source: urlParams.get('gad_source'),
                  gbraid: urlParams.get('gbraid'),
                  wbraid: urlParams.get('wbraid'),
                };

                // Filter out null values
                const filteredUtmData = Object.fromEntries(
                  Object.entries(utmData).filter(([_, value]) => value !== null)
                );

                return {
                  ...ids,
                  measurementId: measurementId,
                  timestamp: Date.now(),
                  landingPage: window.location.href,
                  referrer: document.referrer || undefined,
                  ...filteredUtmData
                };
              } catch (error) {
                console.warn('Failed to capture GA4 session data:', error);
                return {
                  clientId: null,
                  sessionId: null,
                  sessionNumber: null,
                  measurementId: measurementId,
                  timestamp: Date.now(),
                  landingPage: window.location.href,
                  referrer: document.referrer || undefined,
                };
              }
            };

            // Initialize session capture with proper timing
            function initializeGA4SessionCapture() {
              const defaultMeasurementId = 'G-K41XTTG4FC';
              if (!defaultMeasurementId || !defaultMeasurementId.startsWith('G-')) {
                return;
              }

              // Wait a bit for GTM to initialize, then capture
              setTimeout(async function() {
                try {
                  const sessionData = await window.getGa4SessionForCart(defaultMeasurementId);

                  // Store session data globally for use by other components
                  window.__ga4SessionData = sessionData;

                  // Dispatch custom event for components that need this data
                  window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('ga4SessionReady', {
                    detail: sessionData
                  }));

                  if (false) {
                    console.log('GA4 Session Data Captured:', {
                      hasClientId: !!sessionData.clientId,
                      hasSessionId: !!sessionData.sessionId,
                      measurementId: sessionData.measurementId,
                      gtagAvailable: typeof gtag === 'function'
                    });
                  }
                } catch (error) {
                  console.warn('Failed to auto-capture GA4 session:', error);
                }
              }, 2000);
            }

            // Initialize on DOM ready and window load
            if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
              document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initializeGA4SessionCapture);
            } else {
              initializeGA4SessionCapture();
            }

            // Also try on window load as backup
            window.addEventListener('load', function() {
              if (!window.__ga4SessionData) {
                setTimeout(initializeGA4SessionCapture, 1000);
              }
            });

            // Listen for GTM container loaded events
            window.addEventListener('gtm.dom', initializeGA4SessionCapture);
            window.addEventListener('gtm.load', initializeGA4SessionCapture);
